 G'zuz. They were right. I  though  I had  been waiting quite a  while now
 since  my  previous  production. And  I  concidered  1 mounth  as a  long
 period.  Guess  I've  been  perhaps  too   active  they  latest  mounths.
 Well,  we'll  see if that'll  continue in  the future. 1  Mounth. It's no
 time at all! Well, there you go, learning something new every single day.

 I'd like to make all viewers of this production aware of that it consists
 of even more crappy, unimportant (err, nah) information and comments than
 it use to. This due to it's  size. You see, if You have decided to make a
 470k large textfile you can't build it on only ascii-logos, you need some
 a amount of various other parts too. You'll see, if you try it some time!

 `··· ·                                                               · ···'
 Our beloved ascii-scene. And this is what The Suicidal Klown, a.k.a. TSK
 of Sardonyx tells the scene in his co-editorial magazine SeenPoint (issue2)
 about the ascii-artists and the ascii-scene. I quote;

 'Ascii-Artists

  Even if productive, they are lower than swappers and modem traders as
  their function still hasn't been recognised as a real one and very few
  of them (none?) are fulltime Ascii-artists, but when this function will
  be fully recognised they will be placed between sysops and editors.
  (This category is between brackets because numerous sceners consider it
  as unexisting).'

 Listen now, 'None is a fulltime Ascii-artists'? Err? Tell me that again!
 I think that it's time this guy stops checking his mail after mounth-old
 cracks and buys himself an modem instead. 'LOWER than swappers' ... oh,
 yes! I forgot! It takes a hell of a lot of talent to post a pack with
 disks! And you really DO have to be artistic to do it too! 'concider it
 as UNEXISTING' ... my god! Oh yes, what more than 440 persons has releas-
 ed in packs during all times sure must be very 'unexisting' hah?

 And then this TSK/Sdx claims in his 'ladder of value in the scene' that
 EDITING are a position that soon will be as valuable as doing Code,
 Graphics or Music. Oh! Of cause! Typing this, as I just did, really was
 a HARD thing to do. Using my keyboard to write plain info-text IS A FUCK-
 ING UNIMPORTANT, UNARTISTIC, UNTALENTED thing to do, and nothing at all
 to be a single BIT proud of.

 Whatta load of bull! Ascii exists, and appears EVERYWHERE. The whole
 modem-scene probably sees more ascii-logos every day, than they see disk-
 magazines every YEAR.

 Artists! Stand up and show yourself for the 'rest of the scene'. It seems
 like it's needed.
